The advantage of this is that it forces the developer to think of modularity as they develop which makes it easier to update and replace functionality of a certain node by simply swapping it out of the graph. The MixSDK, which relies on Glib and GObject, is portable across operating systems and programming languages. As long as a developer knows how to write a program in one of the language currently supported by the bindings (Python, C and Java), they can hit the ground running and built their own application using the MixSDK. The SDK is written in a Vala which is a language with syntax similar to C# which uses valac (the Vala compiler) that translates Vala source code into C.
